## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of population size P and time t. Classical population dynamics provides numerous ODE models relating growth rate to current population, including density-dependent and time-varying formulations.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth, no density dependence)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth, common in tumor modeling)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population threshold)
- Allee effect (weak/simple): dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 * (1 - c2 * P) (cooperative growth at low density)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (density-dependent with saturating per-capita rate)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (logistic growth minus proportional removal)
- Logistic with constant harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (logistic growth minus constant yield)
- Time-dependent Malthusian: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (exponential growth with time-varying rate)
- Seasonal logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (logistic with periodic environmental forcing)
- Richards growth model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * c3 (generalized growth model)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism vs catabolism balance)
- Power-law growth with saturation: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 / (1 + c2 * P**c3) (generalized density-dependent model)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent regulation → Polynomial in P with negative quadratic term: c0*P - c1*P^2 indicates logistic-type self-limitation
- Allee effects (cooperative dynamics) → Cubic polynomial in P: terms like P*(P-a)*(K-P) indicate bistability with extinction threshold
- Logarithmic per-capita rate → log(K/P) or log-transformed terms indicate Gompertz-type asymmetric growth near carrying capacity
- Seasonal/environmental forcing → Multiplicative periodic modulation sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) on growth terms reflects cyclic resource availability
- Depensation (inverse density dependence) → Fractional powers P^c with 0<c<1 or ratio P/(P+c) for per-capita rate at low densities
- Immigration/emigration terms → Additive constants independent of P represent density-independent population flux
- Predator-prey functional response → Rational forms P/(1+c*P) or P^2/(1+c*P^2) represent saturating consumption/interaction rates
- Time-delayed effects approximated → Explicit time dependence t in growth parameters can proxy for age-structure or delayed feedback
